    FROM [Pxp_Cards] AS [p3]
    WHERE @__ef_filter__p_4 = CAST(1 AS bit) OR [p3].[TenantId] = @__ef_filter__CurrentTenantId_5
) AS [t1] ON [t].[CreditCardId] = [t1].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [Pxp_Flags] AS [p4] ON [t1].[FlagCardId] = [p4].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [Pxp_Subcategories] AS [p5] ON [p0].[Id] = [p5].[CategoryId]
ORDER BY [t].[Date] DESC, [t].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t0].[Id], [p2].[Id], [t1].[Id], [p4].[Id]

INNER JOIN [Pxp_Banks] AS [p1] ON [t].[BankId] = [p1].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Pxp_Flags] AS [p2] ON [p].[FlagCardId] = [p2].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p3].[Id], [p3].[AccountId], [p3].[CategoryId], [p3].[CreationTime], [p3].[CreatorUserId], [p3].[CreditCardId], [p3].[CurrentInstallment], [p3].[Date], [p3].[Description], [p3].[ExpenseValue], [p3].[Installments], [p3].[LastModificationTime], [p3].[LastModifierUserId], [p3].[PaymentTerm], [p3].[PaymentType], [p3].[TenantId], [p3].[TransactionType], [p4].[Id] AS [Id0], [p4].[IconPath], [p4].[IsVisible], [p4].[Name], [p4].[TransactionType] AS [TransactionType0]
    FROM [Pxp_Transactions] AS [p3]
    INNER JOIN [Pxp_Categories] AS [p4] ON [p3].[CategoryId] = [p4].[Id]
    WHERE @__ef_filter__p_2 = CAST(1 AS bit) OR [p3].[TenantId] = @__ef_filter__CurrentTenantId_3
) AS [t0] ON [p].[Id] = [t0].[CreditCardId]
WHERE @__ef_filter__p_0 = CAST(1 AS bit) OR [p].[TenantId] = @__ef_filter__CurrentTenantId_1
ORDER BY [p].[Id], [t].[Id], [p1].[Id], [p2].[Id], [t0].[Id]
